After serving our country, we returned home only to encounter inadequate housing options that didn't meet our needs or reflect the quality of life we deserved.</p>
            <p>We saw the same struggles in our communities - families working multiple jobs just to afford basic housing, veterans living in substandard conditions, and communities suffering from housing instability. We knew there had to be a better way.</p>

As a veteran-owned and operated company, we bring personal understanding and professional expertise to every property we renovate and every family we serve. We're not just in the business of housing - we're in the business of building stronger communities.</p>

    <section class="process-section" aria-labelledby="process-heading">

          <div class="process-step">
            <div class="step-number">1</div>
            <h3>Submit Application</h3>
            <p>Fill out our secure online application form with your housing preferences and voucher information.</p>
          </div>
          <div class="process-step">
            <div class="step-number">2</div>
            <h3>Document Review</h3>

          <div class="process-step">
            <div class="step-number">3</div>

            <p>We'll match you with available properties that meet your needs and budget.</p>
          </div>
          <div class="process-step">

            <h3>Move In</h3>

/* Button Component - Exact Specification */
.btn {
  display: inline-flex;
  align-items: center;
  justify-content: center;
  padding: 0.75rem 1.5rem;
  border-radius: 0.5rem;
  font-weight: 600;
  text-decoration: none;
  transition: all var(--transition-base);
  min-height: 44px;
  cursor: pointer;
  border: none;
  font-size: 1rem;
  position: relative;
}

.btn-loading {
  position: relative;
  pointer-events: none;
}

.spinner {
  width: 16px;
  height: 16px;
  border: 2px solid transparent;
  border-top: 2px solid currentColor;
  border-radius: 50%;
  animation: spin 1s linear infinite;
  margin-right: 0.5rem;
  display: inline-block;
  vertical-align: middle;
}

@keyframes spin {
  0% { transform: rotate(0deg); }
  100% { transform: rotate(360deg); }
}

.btn:hover {
  transform: translateY(-2px);
  box-shadow: 0 10px 20px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
}

.btn-primary {
  background: var(--color-primary-gold);
  color: var(--color-primary-navy);
}

.btn-primary:hover {
  background: var(--color-primary-gold-dark);
  box-shadow: 0 10px 30px rgba(194, 142, 90, 0.3);
}

.btn-secondary {
  background: transparent;
  color: var(--color-primary-navy);
  border: 2px solid var(--color-primary-gold); /* changed from navy to gold */
}

[data-theme="dark"] .btn-secondary {
  color: var(--color-neutral-white);
  border-color: var(--color-primary-gold); /* changed from white to gold */
}

.btn-secondary:hover {
  background: var(--color-primary-navy);
  color: var(--color-neutral-white);
  border-color: var(--color-primary-navy); /* ensures border doesn't stay gold on hover */
}

[data-theme="dark"] .btn-secondary:hover {
  background: var(--color-neutral-white);
  color: var(--color-primary-navy);
  border-color: var(--color-neutral-white); /* ensures border matches background */
}

.btn:disabled {
  opacity: 0.6;
  cursor: not-allowed;
  transform: none;
  box-shadow: none;
}

              <p>To provide dignified, affordable housing solutions for veterans, military families, and working families across East Texas, ensuring that everyone has access to safe, renovated homes they can be proud to call home.</p>
            </div>
            <div class="mission-card">

        <h2 id="story-heading">Our Story</h2>
        <div class="story-content">
          <div class="story-text">
            <p>Properties 4 Creations was founded by veterans who experienced firsthand the housing challenges that many military families and veterans face. After serving our country, we returned home only to encounter inadequate housing options that didn't meet our needs or reflect the quality of life we deserved.</p>
            <p>We saw the same struggles in our communities - families working multiple jobs just to afford basic housing, veterans living in substandard conditions, and communities suffering from housing instability. We knew there had to be a better way.</p>
            <p>That's why we started Properties 4 Creations. As a veteran-owned and operated company, we bring personal understanding and professional expertise to every property we renovate and every family we serve. We're not just in the business of housing - we're in the business of building stronger communities.</p>
          </div>

    <section class="process-section" aria-labelledby="process-heading">
      <div class="container">

        <div class="process-steps">
          <div class="process-step">
            <div class="step-number">1</div>
            <h3>Submit Application</h3>
            <p>Fill out our secure online application form with your housing preferences and voucher information.</p>
          </div>
          <div class="process-step">

              <p>In the meantime, feel free to browse our <a href="/properties/">available properties</a> or learn more <a href="/about/">about our services</a>.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="contact-sidebar">
            <div class="contact-card">
              <h3>Emergency Housing Support</h3>

              <ul class="emergency-contacts">
                <li><strong>Veterans Crisis Line:</strong> <a href="tel:988">988</a></li>
                <li><strong>National Housing Hotline:</strong> <a href="tel:1-800-827-1000">1-800-827-1000</a></li>

              </ul>

        <h2 id="faq-heading" class="sr-only">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
        <div class="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">

          <!-- Application Questions -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="application">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-1" id="faq-header-1" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">How do I apply for housing?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-1" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-1">
              <p>To apply for housing with Properties 4 Creations, simply visit our <a href="/apply/">Apply Now</a> page and fill out our secure online application form. We'll ask for basic information about your housing needs, household size, and voucher type. Our team reviews applications within 24-48 hours and contacts you to discuss available properties that match your requirements.</p>
              <p>We accept both Section 8 and HUD-VASH vouchers, and our veteran-owned company specializes in working with military families and veterans.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="application">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-2" id="faq-header-2" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">Do you accept Section 8 vouchers?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-2" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-2">
              <p>Yes, we proudly accept Section 8 vouchers at all our properties. As a veteran-owned housing provider, we understand the importance of making quality housing accessible to families who need assistance.</p>
              <p>All our properties are Section 8 approved, and we work directly with local housing authorities to ensure a smooth voucher processing experience. We never charge additional fees beyond standard security deposits and rent amounts.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="veterans">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-3" id="faq-header-3" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">What about HUD-VASH for veterans?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-3" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-3">
              <p>We are certified HUD-VASH partners and have dedicated properties specifically designated for veterans with HUD-VASH vouchers. Our veteran-owned company was founded by those who understand the unique housing challenges faced by military families.</p>
              <p>HUD-VASH (Housing and Urban Development - Veterans Affairs Supportive Housing) is a program that combines rental assistance with case management services. We work closely with VA case managers to ensure our veterans receive the comprehensive support they need.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Service Area Questions -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="location">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-4" id="faq-header-4" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">What areas do you serve?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-4" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-4">
              <p>We serve communities across East Texas, with properties in:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Tyler, TX</strong> - Our largest market with the most property options</li>
                <li><strong>Longview, TX</strong> - Historic homes with modern updates</li>
                <li><strong>Marshall, TX</strong> - Rural charm with spacious properties</li>
                <li><strong>Jefferson, TX</strong> - Waterfront properties and ADA-accessible homes</li>
                <li><strong>Kemp & Mineola</strong> - Additional communities in the region</li>
              </ul>
              <p>If you don't see your preferred location listed, contact us to discuss potential expansion or alternative options in nearby areas.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Differentiation Questions -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="general">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-5" id="faq-header-5" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">What makes you different from other housing providers?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-5" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-5">
              <p>As a veteran-owned and operated company, Properties 4 Creations brings unique advantages:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Veteran Understanding:</strong> We understand the specific needs of military families and veterans</li>
                <li><strong>Quality Renovations:</strong> $30k+ invested in each property with premium finishes</li>
                <li><strong>Personal Service:</strong> Direct communication without third-party management companies</li>
                <li><strong>Comprehensive Warranties:</strong> Protection for appliances, systems, and structural elements</li>
                <li><strong>Community Focus:</strong> We invest in East Texas communities and support local veterans</li>
              </ul>
              <p>We're not just landlords - we're neighbors who care about our community's housing stability.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Property Questions -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="properties">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-6" id="faq-header-6" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">Are properties renovated?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-6" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-6">
              <p>Yes, every property undergoes extensive renovations before being offered for rent. Our $30k+ renovation standards include:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Kitchen Updates:</strong> New cabinets, countertops, appliances, and plumbing</li>
                <li><strong>Bathroom Renovations:</strong> Modern fixtures, vanities, and accessibility features</li>
                <li><strong>HVAC Systems:</strong> New heating and cooling systems with warranties</li>
                <li><strong>Exterior Improvements:</strong> Roof repairs, siding updates, and landscaping</li>
                <li><strong>Safety Features:</strong> Updated electrical, smoke detectors, and security systems</li>
              </ul>
              <p>All work is performed by licensed contractors and includes comprehensive warranties for your peace of mind.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Process Questions -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="process">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-7" id="faq-header-7" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">How long does the application take?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-7" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-7">
              <p>Our streamlined process is designed to get you into housing quickly:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Application Review:</strong> 24-48 hours</li>
                <li><strong>Property Matching:</strong> 2-3 business days</li>
                <li><strong>Voucher Processing:</strong> 3-5 business days (varies by program)</li>
                <li><strong>Move-in Ready:</strong> 7-14 days from application approval</li>
              </ul>
              <p>We prioritize urgent housing needs and work to expedite the process for families experiencing homelessness or housing instability. Contact us directly if you need immediate assistance.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="renovations">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-8" id="faq-header-8" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">What's included in renovations?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-8" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-8">
              <p>Our comprehensive renovation package includes everything needed for modern, comfortable living:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Complete Kitchen:</strong> Cabinets, countertops, sink, faucet, appliances</li>
                <li><strong>Updated Bathrooms:</strong> Vanity, mirror, fixtures, exhaust fan</li>
                <li><strong>Flooring:</strong> Durable, easy-to-maintain flooring throughout</li>
                <li><strong>Paint & Finishes:</strong> Fresh paint, trim, and hardware</li>
                <li><strong>HVAC:</strong> New heating and cooling system</li>
                <li><strong>Electrical:</strong> Updated outlets, switches, and lighting</li>
                <li><strong>Plumbing:</strong> Modern fixtures and pressure-balanced valves</li>
                <li><strong>Exterior:</strong> Roof, windows, doors, and landscaping</li>
              </ul>
              <p>Each renovation is customized to the property while maintaining our quality standards.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Pets and Requirements -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="pets">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-9" id="faq-header-9" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">Do you allow pets?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-9" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-9">
              <p>Yes, we welcome pets at most of our properties! Our pet policy includes:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Pet Deposit:</strong> $300 (refundable with proper care of the property)</li>
                <li><strong>Monthly Pet Rent:</strong> $25 per pet</li>
                <li><strong>Size Limit:</strong> No weight restrictions for service animals</li>
                <li><strong>Breed Restrictions:</strong> None for service animals; case-by-case for others</li>
              </ul>
              <p>Service animals and emotional support animals are always welcome with proper documentation. We understand pets are family members and work to accommodate responsible pet owners.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="requirements">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-10" id="faq-header-10" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">What are your income requirements?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-10" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-10">
              <p>Income requirements vary based on your voucher program and household size:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Section 8:</strong> Must meet program income limits (typically 30-50% of area median income)</li>
                <li><strong>HUD-VASH:</strong> Determined by VA case manager and program guidelines</li>
                <li><strong>Market Rate:</strong> 2.5x monthly rent minimum (may be flexible for qualified applicants)</li>
              </ul>
              <p>We work with various income sources including employment, disability benefits, Social Security, and veterans benefits. Our team can help you understand eligibility and explore assistance programs that may help bridge any gaps.</p>
              <p>Contact us to discuss your specific situation - we may have additional resources or alternative options available.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

        </div>

        <h2 id="standards-heading" class="text-center">Our Renovation Standards</h2>
        <div class="standards-content">
          <div class="standards-text">
            <p>Every property undergoes our comprehensive $30k+ renovation process, ensuring that each home meets modern standards for safety, comfort, and functionality.</p>

            <h3>Safety & Accessibility</h3>
            <ul>
              <li>Updated electrical systems with modern outlets and GFCI protection</li>
              <li>ADA-compliant accessibility features in bathrooms and entryways</li>
              <li>Smoke and carbon monoxide detectors with battery backup</li>
              <li>Reinforced structural elements for long-term stability</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Modern Comfort</h3>
            <ul>
              <li>Energy-efficient HVAC systems with programmable thermostats</li>
              <li>Insulated walls and ceilings for year-round comfort</li>
              <li>Modern plumbing with pressure-balanced faucets</li>
              <li>Quality flooring that stands up to family life</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Quality Finishes</h3>
            <ul>
              <li>Premium appliances with full warranties</li>
              <li>Granite or quartz countertops in kitchens</li>
              <li>Custom cabinetry with soft-close hinges</li>
              <li>Professional paint and trim throughout</li>
            </ul>
          </div>

    <section class="hero hero-privacy" aria-labelledby="hero-heading">
      <div class="container">
        <h1 id="hero-heading">Privacy Policy</h1>
        <p>Your privacy and data security are important to us. Learn how we collect, use, and protect your personal information.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <!-- Privacy Policy Content -->
    <section class="privacy-content" aria-labelledby="privacy-heading">
      <div class="container">
        <h2 id="privacy-heading" class="sr-only">Privacy Policy Details</h2>

        <div class="policy-content">
          <div class="policy-section">
            <h2>Overview</h2>
            <p>Properties 4 Creations ("we," "us," or "our") is committed to protecting your privacy. This Privacy Policy explains how we collect, use, disclose, and safeguard your information when you visit our website or use our housing services.</p>
            <p>By using our website or submitting an application, you agree to the collection and use of information in accordance with this policy.</p>
          </div>

          <div class="policy-section">
            <h2>Information We Collect</h2>

            <h3>Personal Information</h3>
            <p>We may collect the following types of personal information:</p>
            <ul>
              <li><strong>Contact Information:</strong> Name, email address, phone number, mailing address</li>
              <li><strong>Housing Information:</strong> Household size, income information, housing voucher details, preferred property types</li>
              <li><strong>Identification Information:</strong> Date of birth, Social Security number (for voucher verification only)</li>
              <li><strong>Emergency Contact:</strong> Names and contact information for emergency contacts</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Automatically Collected Information</h3>
            <p>When you visit our website, we may automatically collect:</p>
            <ul>
              <li><strong>Usage Data:</strong> Pages visited, time spent on pages, click patterns</li>
              <li><strong>Device Information:</strong> IP address, browser type, operating system, screen resolution</li>
              <li><strong>Cookies and Tracking:</strong> Information about your preferences and website usage</li>
            </ul>
          </div>

          <div class="policy-section">
            <h2>How We Use Your Information</h2>
            <p>We use the information we collect for the following purposes:</p>

            <h3>Housing Services</h3>
            <ul>
              <li>Process housing applications and verify eligibility</li>
              <li>Match applicants with available properties</li>
              <li>Communicate about application status and property availability</li>
              <li>Verify housing voucher information with relevant agencies</li>
              <li>Provide property tours and leasing services</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Communication</h3>
            <ul>
              <li>Respond to inquiries and provide customer support</li>
              <li>Send important updates about your application or tenancy</li>
              <li>Provide information about new properties or services</li>
              <li>Send newsletters or housing resource information (with consent)</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Legal and Safety</h3>
            <ul>
              <li>Comply with fair housing laws and regulations</li>
              <li>Conduct background checks and reference verification</li>
              <li>Prevent fraud and ensure housing stability</li>
              <li>Meet legal obligations and respond to legal requests</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Website Improvement</h3>
            <ul>
              <li>Analyze website usage and improve user experience</li>
              <li>Maintain website security and prevent unauthorized access</li>
              <li>Customize content and services based on preferences</li>
            </ul>
          </div>

          <div class="policy-section">
            <h2>Information Sharing</h2>
            <p>We do not sell, trade, or rent your personal information to third parties. We may share your information only in the following circumstances:</p>

            <h3>With Your Consent</h3>
            <p>We share information when you explicitly consent to the sharing.</p>

            <h3>Service Providers</h3>
            <p>We may share information with trusted third-party service providers who assist us with:</p>
            <ul>
              <li>Background check services</li>
              <li>Credit reporting agencies</li>
              <li>Housing voucher verification</li>
              <li>Property management systems</li>
              <li>Website hosting and maintenance</li>
            </ul>
            <p>These providers are contractually obligated to protect your information and use it only for authorized purposes.</p>

            <h3>Government Agencies</h3>
            <p>We may share information with government agencies when required by law or to verify:</p>
            <ul>
              <li>Housing voucher eligibility</li>
              <li>Income and employment information</li>
              <li>Criminal background (where legally permitted)</li>
              <li>Fair housing compliance</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Legal Requirements</h3>
            <p>We may disclose information if required by law, court order, or government regulation, or to protect our rights, property, or safety.</p>
          </div>

          <div class="policy-section">
            <h2>Data Security</h2>
            <p>We implement appropriate technical and organizational security measures to protect your personal information:</p>

            <h3>Security Measures</h3>
            <ul>
              <li>SSL/TLS encryption for all data transmission</li>
              <li>Secure data storage with access controls</li>
              <li>Regular security audits and updates</li>
              <li>Employee training on data protection</li>
              <li>Secure disposal of physical and electronic records</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Data Retention</h3>
            <p>We retain your information only as long as necessary for the purposes outlined in this policy:</p>
            <ul>
              <li>Application records: 7 years (as required by fair housing laws)</li>
              <li>Active tenant records: Duration of tenancy plus 7 years</li>
              <li>Website analytics: 2 years</li>
              <li>Inactive accounts: 3 years before deletion</li>
            </ul>
          </div>

          <div class="policy-section">
            <h2>Your Privacy Rights</h2>
            <p>You have certain rights regarding your personal information:</p>

            <h3>Access and Correction</h3>
            <p>You have the right to:</p>
            <ul>
              <li>Access the personal information we hold about you</li>
              <li>Request correction of inaccurate or incomplete information</li>
              <li>Receive a copy of your information in a portable format</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Deletion and Restriction</h3>
            <p>You have the right to:</p>
            <ul>
              <li>Request deletion of your personal information</li>
              <li>Restrict processing of your information in certain circumstances</li>
              <li>Object to processing based on legitimate interests</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Withdraw Consent</h3>
            <p>You may withdraw consent for marketing communications at any time by contacting us or using the unsubscribe link in our emails.</p>

            <h3>How to Exercise Your Rights</h3>
            <p>To exercise any of these rights, please contact us:</p>
            <ul>
              <li><strong>Email:</strong> <a href="mailto:info@properties4creations.com">info@properties4creations.com</a></li>
              <li><strong>Phone:</strong> <a href="tel:903-555-1234">(903) 555-1234</a></li>
              <li><strong>Mail:</strong> Properties 4 Creations, Privacy Officer, Tyler, TX 75701</li>
            </ul>
          </div>

          <div class="policy-section">
            <h2>Cookies and Tracking</h2>
            <p>Our website uses cookies and similar technologies to enhance your experience:</p>

            <h3>Essential Cookies</h3>
            <p>Required for website functionality, including:</p>
            <ul>
              <li>Session management and security</li>
              <li>Form data preservation</li>
              <li>Accessibility preferences</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Analytics Cookies</h3>
            <p>Help us understand website usage to improve services:</p>
            <ul>
              <li>Pages visited and time spent</li>
              <li>Traffic sources and user behavior</li>
              <li>Device and browser information</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Preference Cookies</h3>
            <p>Remember your choices and preferences:</p>
            <ul>
              <li>Dark mode selection</li>
              <li>Language preferences</li>
              <li>Form data (temporary)</li>
            </ul>

            <p>You can control cookie settings through your browser preferences. However, disabling certain cookies may affect website functionality.</p>
          </div>

          <div class="policy-section">
            <h2>Third-Party Links</h2>
            <p>Our website may contain links to third-party websites and services. This Privacy Policy does not apply to these external sites. We encourage you to review the privacy policies of any third-party services you use.</p>
          </div>

          <div class="policy-section">
            <h2>Children's Privacy</h2>
            <p>Our services are intended for adults. We do not knowingly collect personal information from children under 13. If we become aware that we have collected information from a child under 13, we will take steps to delete such information.</p>
          </div>

          <div class="policy-section">
            <h2>Changes to This Policy</h2>
            <p>We may update this Privacy Policy from time to time. We will notify you of any material changes by:</p>
            <ul>
              <li>Posting the updated policy on our website</li>
              <li>Sending an email notification</li>
              <li>Providing notice through our application portal</li>
            </ul>
            <p>Your continued use of our services after changes take effect constitutes acceptance of the updated policy.</p>
          </div>

          <div class="policy-section">
            <h2>Contact Us</h2>
            <p>If you have questions about this Privacy Policy or our data practices, please contact us:</p>

            <div class="contact-info">
              <p><strong>Properties 4 Creations</strong></p>
              <p><strong>Privacy Officer</strong></p>
              <p><strong>Phone:</strong> <a href="tel:903-555-1234">(903) 555-1234</a></p>
              <p><strong>Email:</strong> <a href="mailto:info@properties4creations.com">info@properties4creations.com</a></p>
              <p><strong>Address:</strong> Properties 4 Creations<br>
              Tyler, TX 75701</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="policy-footer">
            <p><strong>Last Updated:</strong> December 26, 2025</p>
            <p><strong>Effective Date:</strong> December 26, 2025</p>
          </div>

      <div class="container">
        <h1 id="hero-heading">Housing Resources</h1>
        <p>Comprehensive guide to housing assistance programs, veteran benefits, and local support services in East Texas.</p>
      </div>
    </section>

    <!-- Resource Categories -->
    <section class="resources-section" aria-labelledby="resources-heading">
      <div class="container">
        <h2 id="resources-heading" class="sr-only">Housing Resources</h2>

        <!-- HUD Housing Resources -->
        <div class="resource-category">
          <h2>HUD Housing Resources</h2>
          <p>The U.S. Department of Housing and Urban Development provides comprehensive housing assistance programs.</p>

          <div class="resources-grid">
            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>HUD.gov</h3>
              <p>Official U.S. Department of Housing and Urban Development website with comprehensive housing information.</p>
              <a href="https://www.hud.gov/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">Visit HUD.gov</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Section 8 Program</h3>
              <p>Learn about the Housing Choice Vouchers (Section 8) program, eligibility requirements, and how to apply.</p>
              <a href="https://www.hud.gov/program_offices/public_indian_housing/programs/hcv" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">Section 8 Information</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>HUD-VASH Program</h3>
              <p>HUD-Veterans Affairs Supportive Housing program combining rental assistance with VA case management.</p>
              <a href="https://www.hud.gov/program_offices/public_indian_housing/programs/hcv/vash" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">HUD-VASH Details</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Fair Housing</h3>
              <p>Information about fair housing laws, discrimination prevention, and your rights as a housing applicant.</p>
              <a href="https://www.hud.gov/program_offices/fair_housing_equal_opp" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">Fair Housing Resources</a>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- VA Housing Assistance -->
        <div class="resource-category">
          <h2>VA Housing Assistance</h2>
          <p>Dedicated housing programs and support services for veterans and their families.</p>

          <div class="resources-grid">
            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>VA.gov Housing</h3>
              <p>Official Department of Veterans Affairs housing assistance programs and application information.</p>
              <a href="https://www.va.gov/housing-assistance/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">VA Housing Assistance</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Veterans Crisis Line</h3>
              <p>24/7 confidential support for veterans in crisis, including housing instability and homelessness.</p>
              <a href="tel:988" class="resource-link">Call 988</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>VA Case Management</h3>
              <p>Connect with VA case managers for personalized housing assistance and supportive services.</p>
              <a href="https://www.va.gov/homeless/ssvf/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">SSVF Program</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>VA Loan Programs</h3>
              <p>VA guaranteed home loans for eligible veterans, including purchase and refinance options.</p>
              <a href="https://www.va.gov/housing-assistance/home-loans/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">VA Loan Information</a>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Section 8 Information -->
        <div class="resource-category">
          <h2>Section 8 & Voucher Programs</h2>
          <p>Detailed information about housing choice vouchers and local program administration.</p>

          <div class="resources-grid">
            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>How Section 8 Works</h3>
              <p>Complete guide to the Section 8 Housing Choice Voucher program, including application process and tenant responsibilities.</p>
              <a href="https://www.hud.gov/topics/rental_assistance/phprog" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">Program Guide</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Voucher Eligibility</h3>
              <p>Income limits, family size requirements, and other eligibility criteria for Section 8 assistance.</p>
              <a href="https://www.hud.gov/states/texas/renting" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">Eligibility Information</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Finding Housing</h3>
              <p>Tips for finding Section 8 approved housing and working with property owners who accept vouchers.</p>
              <a href="https://www.hud.gov/states/texas/renting/section8" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">Housing Search Guide</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Landlord Resources</h3>
              <p>Information for property owners interested in participating in the Section 8 program.</p>
              <a href="https://www.hud.gov/program_offices/public_indian_housing/pha/contacts" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">Landlord Information</a>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Veteran Benefits -->
        <div class="resource-category">

            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Veterans Employment</h3>
              <p>Job training, placement services, and employment resources for transitioning service members.</p>
              <a href="https://www.dol.gov/agencies/vets" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">Veterans Employment</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Veterans Organizations</h3>

          </div>
        </div>

        <!-- Local Housing Authorities -->
        <div class="resource-category">

        <!-- Financial Assistance Programs -->
        <div class="resource-category">
          <h2>Financial Assistance Programs</h2>
          <p>Additional financial support programs that can help with housing costs and stability.</p>

          <div class="resources-grid">
            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Utility Assistance</h3>
              <p>Programs to help with utility costs including electricity, water, and heating assistance.</p>
              <a href="https://www.hud.gov/states/texas/renting/utility" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">Utility Assistance Programs</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Emergency Rental Assistance</h3>
              <p>Temporary rental assistance for families experiencing financial hardship or homelessness.</p>
              <a href="https://www.hud.gov/states/texas/renting/era" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">ERA Program</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Food & Nutrition Programs</h3>
              <p>SNAP benefits and other nutrition assistance programs that can free up funds for housing.</p>
              <a href="https://www.hud.gov/states/texas/renting/snap" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="resource-link">SNAP Information</a>
            </div>

            <div class="resource-card">
              <h3>Legal Aid Services</h3>
              <p>Free legal assistance for housing-related issues including eviction prevention and tenant rights.</p>

            </div>

      </div>

    <!-- FAQ Search -->
    <section class="faq-search-section" aria-labelledby="search-heading">

    <!-- FAQ Accordion -->
    <section class="faq-section" aria-labelledby="faq-heading">
      <div class="container">
        <h2 id="faq-heading" class="sr-only">Frequently Asked Questions</h2>
        <div class="accordion" role="tablist" aria-multiselectable="true">

          <!-- Application Questions -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="application">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-1" id="faq-header-1" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">How do I apply for housing?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-1" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-1">
              <p>To apply for housing with Properties 4 Creations, simply visit our <a href="/apply/">Apply Now</a> page and fill out our secure online application form. We'll ask for basic information about your housing needs, household size, and voucher type. Our team reviews applications within 24-48 hours and contacts you to discuss available properties that match your requirements.</p>
              <p>We accept both Section 8 and HUD-VASH vouchers, and our veteran-owned company specializes in working with military families and veterans.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="application">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-2" id="faq-header-2" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">Do you accept Section 8 vouchers?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-2" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-2">
              <p>Yes, we proudly accept Section 8 vouchers at all our properties. As a veteran-owned housing provider, we understand the importance of making quality housing accessible to families who need assistance.</p>
              <p>All our properties are Section 8 approved, and we work directly with local housing authorities to ensure a smooth voucher processing experience. We never charge additional fees beyond standard security deposits and rent amounts.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="veterans">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-3" id="faq-header-3" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">What about HUD-VASH for veterans?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-3" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-3">
              <p>We are certified HUD-VASH partners and have dedicated properties specifically designated for veterans with HUD-VASH vouchers. Our veteran-owned company was founded by those who understand the unique housing challenges faced by military families.</p>
              <p>HUD-VASH (Housing and Urban Development - Veterans Affairs Supportive Housing) is a program that combines rental assistance with case management services. We work closely with VA case managers to ensure our veterans receive the comprehensive support they need.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Service Area Questions -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="location">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-4" id="faq-header-4" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">What areas do you serve?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-4" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-4">
              <p>We serve communities across East Texas, with properties in:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Tyler, TX</strong> - Our largest market with the most property options</li>
                <li><strong>Longview, TX</strong> - Historic homes with modern updates</li>
                <li><strong>Marshall, TX</strong> - Rural charm with spacious properties</li>
                <li><strong>Jefferson, TX</strong> - Waterfront properties and ADA-accessible homes</li>
                <li><strong>Kemp & Mineola</strong> - Additional communities in the region</li>
              </ul>
              <p>If you don't see your preferred location listed, contact us to discuss potential expansion or alternative options in nearby areas.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Differentiation Questions -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="general">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-5" id="faq-header-5" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">What makes you different from other housing providers?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-5" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-5">
              <p>As a veteran-owned and operated company, Properties 4 Creations brings unique advantages:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Veteran Understanding:</strong> We understand the specific needs of military families and veterans</li>
                <li><strong>Quality Renovations:</strong> $30k+ invested in each property with premium finishes</li>
                <li><strong>Personal Service:</strong> Direct communication without third-party management companies</li>
                <li><strong>Comprehensive Warranties:</strong> Protection for appliances, systems, and structural elements</li>
                <li><strong>Community Focus:</strong> We invest in East Texas communities and support local veterans</li>
              </ul>
              <p>We're not just landlords - we're neighbors who care about our community's housing stability.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Property Questions -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="properties">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-6" id="faq-header-6" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">Are properties renovated?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-6" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-6">
              <p>Yes, every property undergoes extensive renovations before being offered for rent. Our $30k+ renovation standards include:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Kitchen Updates:</strong> New cabinets, countertops, appliances, and plumbing</li>
                <li><strong>Bathroom Renovations:</strong> Modern fixtures, vanities, and accessibility features</li>
                <li><strong>HVAC Systems:</strong> New heating and cooling systems with warranties</li>
                <li><strong>Exterior Improvements:</strong> Roof repairs, siding updates, and landscaping</li>
                <li><strong>Safety Features:</strong> Updated electrical, smoke detectors, and security systems</li>
              </ul>
              <p>All work is performed by licensed contractors and includes comprehensive warranties for your peace of mind.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Process Questions -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="process">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-7" id="faq-header-7" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">How long does the application take?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-7" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-7">
              <p>Our streamlined process is designed to get you into housing quickly:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Application Review:</strong> 24-48 hours</li>
                <li><strong>Property Matching:</strong> 2-3 business days</li>
                <li><strong>Voucher Processing:</strong> 3-5 business days (varies by program)</li>
                <li><strong>Move-in Ready:</strong> 7-14 days from application approval</li>
              </ul>
              <p>We prioritize urgent housing needs and work to expedite the process for families experiencing homelessness or housing instability. Contact us directly if you need immediate assistance.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="renovations">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-8" id="faq-header-8" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">What's included in renovations?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-8" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-8">
              <p>Our comprehensive renovation package includes everything needed for modern, comfortable living:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Complete Kitchen:</strong> Cabinets, countertops, sink, faucet, appliances</li>
                <li><strong>Updated Bathrooms:</strong> Vanity, mirror, fixtures, exhaust fan</li>
                <li><strong>Flooring:</strong> Durable, easy-to-maintain flooring throughout</li>
                <li><strong>Paint & Finishes:</strong> Fresh paint, trim, and hardware</li>
                <li><strong>HVAC:</strong> New heating and cooling system</li>
                <li><strong>Electrical:</strong> Updated outlets, switches, and lighting</li>
                <li><strong>Plumbing:</strong> Modern fixtures and pressure-balanced valves</li>
                <li><strong>Exterior:</strong> Roof, windows, doors, and landscaping</li>
              </ul>
              <p>Each renovation is customized to the property while maintaining our quality standards.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <!-- Pets and Requirements -->
          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="pets">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-9" id="faq-header-9" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">Do you allow pets?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-9" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-9">
              <p>Yes, we welcome pets at most of our properties! Our pet policy includes:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Pet Deposit:</strong> $300 (refundable with proper care of the property)</li>
                <li><strong>Monthly Pet Rent:</strong> $25 per pet</li>
                <li><strong>Size Limit:</strong> No weight restrictions for service animals</li>
                <li><strong>Breed Restrictions:</strong> None for service animals; case-by-case for others</li>
              </ul>
              <p>Service animals and emotional support animals are always welcome with proper documentation. We understand pets are family members and work to accommodate responsible pet owners.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="accordion-item" data-category="requirements">
            <button class="accordion-header" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="faq-10" id="faq-header-10" role="tab">
              <span class="question-text">What are your income requirements?</span>
              <span class="accordion-icon" aria-hidden="true">+</span>
            </button>
            <div class="accordion-content" id="faq-10" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="faq-header-10">
              <p>Income requirements vary based on your voucher program and household size:</p>
              <ul>
                <li><strong>Section 8:</strong> Must meet program income limits (typically 30-50% of area median income)</li>
                <li><strong>HUD-VASH:</strong> Determined by VA case manager and program guidelines</li>
                <li><strong>Market Rate:</strong> 2.5x monthly rent minimum (may be flexible for qualified applicants)</li>
              </ul>
              <p>We work with various income sources including employment, disability benefits, Social Security, and veterans benefits. Our team can help you understand eligibility and explore assistance programs that may help bridge any gaps.</p>
              <p>Contact us to discuss your specific situation - we may have additional resources or alternative options available.</p>
            </div>
          </div>

        </div>

        <!-- No Results Message -->

          <h3>No questions found</h3>
          <p>Try different search terms or <a href="/contact/">contact us</a> directly with your question.</p>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>

    <!-- Renovation Standards -->
    <section class="standards-section" aria-labelledby="standards-heading">
      <div class="container">
        <h2 id="standards-heading" class="text-center">Our Renovation Standards</h2>
        <div class="standards-content">
          <div class="standards-text">
            <p>Every property undergoes our comprehensive $30k+ renovation process, ensuring that each home meets modern standards for safety, comfort, and functionality.</p>

            <h3>Safety & Accessibility</h3>
            <ul>
              <li>Updated electrical systems with modern outlets and GFCI protection</li>
              <li>ADA-compliant accessibility features in bathrooms and entryways</li>
              <li>Smoke and carbon monoxide detectors with battery backup</li>
              <li>Reinforced structural elements for long-term stability</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Modern Comfort</h3>
            <ul>
              <li>Energy-efficient HVAC systems with programmable thermostats</li>
              <li>Insulated walls and ceilings for year-round comfort</li>
              <li>Modern plumbing with pressure-balanced faucets</li>
              <li>Quality flooring that stands up to family life</li>
            </ul>

            <h3>Quality Finishes</h3>
            <ul>
              <li>Premium appliances with full warranties</li>
              <li>Granite or quartz countertops in kitchens</li>
              <li>Custom cabinetry with soft-close hinges</li>
              <li>Professional paint and trim throughout</li>
            </ul>

/**
 * Properties 4 Creations - Accessibility Module
 * Handles accessibility features and focus management
 *
 * @fileoverview Provides accessibility enhancements and focus management
 * @author Properties 4 Creations
 */

/**
 * Add focus management for better keyboard navigation
 */
export function initFocusManagement() {
  // Trap focus in mobile menu when open
  const menuToggle = document.querySelector('.menu-toggle');
  const mainNav = document.querySelector('.main-navigation');

  if (menuToggle && mainNav) {
    menuToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const isOpen = menuToggle.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true';

      if (isOpen) {
        // Focus first menu item
        const firstLink = mainNav.querySelector('.nav-link');
        if (firstLink) {
          setTimeout(() => firstLink.focus(), 100);
        }
      }
    });
  }

  // Close mobile menu on escape
  document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
    if (e.key === 'Escape') {
      const menuToggle = document.querySelector('.menu-toggle');
      if (menuToggle && menuToggle.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true') {
        menuToggle.click();
        menuToggle.focus();
      }
    }
  });
}

/**
 * Set current page indicator in navigation
 */
export function setCurrentPage() {
  const currentPath = window.location.pathname;

  // Remove trailing slash for comparison
  const normalizedPath = currentPath.replace(/\/$/, '') || '/';

  const navLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.nav-link');

  navLinks.forEach(link => {
    const linkHref = link.getAttribute('href');

    if (linkHref === normalizedPath) {
      link.classList.add('is-active');
    } else {
      link.classList.remove('is-active');
    }
  });
}

/**
 * Normalize path for comparison
 * @param {string} path - The path to normalize
 * @returns {string} Normalized path
 */
export function normalizePath(path) {
  return path.replace(/index\.html$/, '').replace(/\/$/, '') || '/';
}

/**
 * Announce message to screen readers
 * @param {string} message - The message to announce
 */
export function announceToScreenReader(message) {
  const announcement = document.createElement('div');
  announcement.setAttribute('aria-live', 'polite');
  announcement.setAttribute('aria-atomic', 'true');
  announcement.className = 'sr-only';
  announcement.textContent = message;

  document.body.appendChild(announcement);

  // Remove after announcement
  setTimeout(() => {
    if (announcement.parentNode) {
      announcement.remove();
    }
  }, 1000);
}

/**
 * Properties 4 Creations - FAQ Module
 * Handles FAQ accordion functionality and search
 *
 * @fileoverview Provides FAQ accordion and search functionality
 * @author Properties 4 Creations
 */

/**
 * Initialize FAQ accordions
 */
export function initFAQ() {
  initializeAccordions();
  initializeFAQSearch();
}

/**
 * Initialize accordions (FAQ section)
 */
function initializeAccordions() {
  const accordionHeaders = document.querySelectorAll('.accordion-header');

  accordionHeaders.forEach(header => {
    header.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const content = header.nextElementSibling;
      const isActive = content.classList.contains('active');

      // Close all accordions in the same group
      const accordion = header.closest('.accordion');
      const allContents = accordion.querySelectorAll('.accordion-content');
      const allHeaders = accordion.querySelectorAll('.accordion-header');

      allContents.forEach(c => {
        c.classList.remove('active');
        c.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
      });
      allHeaders.forEach(h => h.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false'));

      // Open clicked accordion if it wasn't active
      if (!isActive) {
        content.classList.add('active');
        header.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'true');
        content.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
      }
    });

    // Set initial ARIA attributes
    header.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');
    const content = header.nextElementSibling;
    content.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
  });
}

/**
 * Initialize FAQ search functionality
 */
function initializeFAQSearch() {
  const searchInput = document.getElementById('faq-search');
  const clearButton = document.getElementById('clear-search');
  const noResults = document.getElementById('faq-no-results');

  if (!searchInput) return;

  // Add search functionality
  searchInput.addEventListener('input', debounce(handleFAQSearch, 300));

  // Clear search functionality
  if (clearButton) {
    clearButton.addEventListener('click', clearFAQSearch);
  }

  // Keyboard shortcuts
  searchInput.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
    if (e.key === 'Escape') {
      clearFAQSearch();
    }
  });
}

/**
 * Handle FAQ search
 */
function handleFAQSearch() {
  const searchInput = document.getElementById('faq-search');
  const clearButton = document.getElementById('clear-search');
  const noResults = document.getElementById('faq-no-results');
  const searchTerm = searchInput.value.toLowerCase().trim();

  const accordionItems = document.querySelectorAll('.accordion-item');
  let visibleCount = 0;

  accordionItems.forEach(item => {
    const question = item.querySelector('.question-text');
    const answer = item.querySelector('.accordion-content');
    const category = item.dataset.category || '';

    if (!question || !answer) return;

    const questionText = question.textContent.toLowerCase();
    const answerText = answer.textContent.toLowerCase();

    const matches = !searchTerm ||
      questionText.includes(searchTerm) ||
      answerText.includes(searchTerm) ||
      category.includes(searchTerm);

    if (matches) {
      item.style.display = 'block';
      visibleCount++;
    } else {
      item.style.display = 'none';
    }
  });

  // Show/hide clear button
  if (clearButton) {
    clearButton.style.display = searchTerm ? 'inline-block' : 'none';
  }

  // Show/hide no results message
  if (noResults) {
    noResults.style.display = visibleCount === 0 && searchTerm ? 'block' : 'none';
  }

  // Announce results to screen readers
  if (searchTerm) {
    const announcement = `${visibleCount} FAQ items found for "${searchTerm}"`;
    announceToScreenReader(announcement);
  }
}

/**
 * Clear FAQ search
 */
function clearFAQSearch() {
  const searchInput = document.getElementById('faq-search');
  const clearButton = document.getElementById('clear-search');
  const noResults = document.getElementById('faq-no-results');

  if (searchInput) searchInput.value = '';
  if (clearButton) clearButton.style.display = 'none';
  if (noResults) noResults.style.display = 'none';

  // Show all FAQ items
  const accordionItems = document.querySelectorAll('.accordion-item');
  accordionItems.forEach(item => {
    item.style.display = 'block';
  });

  // Close all accordions
  const accordionContents = document.querySelectorAll('.accordion-content');
  const accordionHeaders = document.querySelectorAll('.accordion-header');
  accordionContents.forEach(content => content.classList.remove('active'));
  accordionHeaders.forEach(header => header.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false'));
}

/**
 * Announce message to screen readers
 */
function announceToScreenReader(message) {
  const announcement = document.createElement('div');
  announcement.setAttribute('aria-live', 'polite');
  announcement.setAttribute('aria-atomic', 'true');
  announcement.className = 'sr-only';
  announcement.textContent = message;

  document.body.appendChild(announcement);

  // Remove after announcement
  setTimeout(() => {
    if (announcement.parentNode) {
      announcement.remove();
    }
  }, 1000);
}

/**
 * Utility function to debounce function calls
 */
function debounce(func, wait) {
  let timeout;
  return function executedFunction(...args) {
    const later = () => {
      clearTimeout(timeout);
      func(...args);
    };
    clearTimeout(timeout);
    timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
  };
}

// Properties 4 Creations - Comparison Slider
// Handles before/after image comparison functionality

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  window.comparisonSlider.initialize();
});

/**
 * Initialize all comparison sliders on the page
 */
function initializeComparisonSliders() {
  const sliders = document.querySelectorAll('.comparison-slider');

  sliders.forEach((slider, index) => {
    createComparisonSlider(slider, index);
  });
}

/**
 * Create a comparison slider for a given container
 * Supports both pre-rendered images and data attributes
 */
function createComparisonSlider(container, index) {
  const beforeImage = container.querySelector('.before-image');
  const afterImage = container.querySelector('.after-image');
  const beforeSrc = container.dataset.before;
  const afterSrc = container.dataset.after;

  // Handle data attribute pattern (Impact Gallery style)
  if (beforeSrc && afterSrc) {
    // Create the slider structure for data attributes
    container.innerHTML = `
      <img src="${beforeSrc}" alt="Before renovation" class="before-image" style="display: block;">
      <div class="slider-overlay" style="background-image: url('${afterSrc}')"></div>
      <div class="slider-handle" role="slider" aria-label="Adjust before/after comparison" aria-valuemin="0" aria-valuemax="100" aria-valuenow="50" tabindex="0">
        <div class="slider-handle-button" aria-label="Drag to compare images"></div>
      </div>
      <div class="slider-label before-label">Before</div>
      <div class="slider-label after-label">After</div>
    `;
  }
  // Handle pre-rendered image pattern
  else if (!beforeImage || !afterImage) {
    console.warn('Comparison slider missing before or after image');
    return;
  }

  const finalBeforeImage = container.querySelector('.before-image');
  const finalAfterImage = container.querySelector('.after-image');
  const overlay = container.querySelector('.slider-overlay');
  const handle = container.querySelector('.slider-handle');

  if (!finalBeforeImage || !overlay || !handle) {
    console.warn('Comparison slider elements not created properly');
    return;
  }

  // Position images
  container.style.position = 'relative';
  finalBeforeImage.style.position = 'absolute';
  finalBeforeImage.style.top = '0';
  finalBeforeImage.style.left = '0';
  finalBeforeImage.style.width = '100%';
  finalBeforeImage.style.height = '100%';
  finalBeforeImage.style.objectFit = 'cover';

  overlay.style.position = 'absolute';
  overlay.style.top = '0';
  overlay.style.left = '0';
  overlay.style.width = '50%';
  overlay.style.height = '100%';
  overlay.style.backgroundSize = 'cover';
  overlay.style.backgroundPosition = 'center';
  overlay.style.backgroundRepeat = 'no-repeat';

  handle.style.position = 'absolute';
  handle.style.top = '50%';
  handle.style.left = '50%';
  handle.style.transform = 'translate(-50%, -50%)';
  handle.style.zIndex = '10';
  handle.style.cursor = 'ew-resize';

  // Initialize slider position
  let sliderPosition = 50; // percentage
  updateSlider(sliderPosition, container, overlay, handle);

  // Mouse events
  let isDragging = false;

  handle.addEventListener('mousedown', (e) => {
    isDragging = true;
    handle.style.cursor = 'grabbing';
    e.preventDefault();
  });

  document.addEventListener('mousemove', (e) => {
    if (!isDragging) return;

    const rect = container.getBoundingClientRect();
    const x = e.clientX - rect.left;
    const percentage = (x / rect.width) * 100;

    sliderPosition = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, percentage));
    updateSlider(sliderPosition, container, overlay, handle);
  });

  document.addEventListener('mouseup', () => {
    if (isDragging) {
      isDragging = false;
      handle.style.cursor = 'ew-resize';
    }
  });

  // Touch events for mobile
  handle.addEventListener('touchstart', (e) => {
    isDragging = true;
    e.preventDefault();
  });

  document.addEventListener('touchmove', (e) => {
    if (!isDragging) return;

    const rect = container.getBoundingClientRect();
    const touch = e.touches[0];
    const x = touch.clientX - rect.left;
    const percentage = (x / rect.width) * 100;

    sliderPosition = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, percentage));
    updateSlider(sliderPosition, container, overlay, handle);
  });

  document.addEventListener('touchend', () => {
    isDragging = false;
  });

  // Keyboard navigation
  handle.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
    const step = 5; // 5% steps

    switch (e.key) {
      case 'ArrowLeft':
        sliderPosition = Math.max(0, sliderPosition - step);
        updateSlider(sliderPosition, container, overlay, handle);
        e.preventDefault();
        break;
      case 'ArrowRight':
        sliderPosition = Math.min(100, sliderPosition + step);
        updateSlider(sliderPosition, container, overlay, handle);
        e.preventDefault();
        break;
      case 'Home':
        sliderPosition = 0;
        updateSlider(sliderPosition, container, overlay, handle);
        e.preventDefault();
        break;
      case 'End':
        sliderPosition = 100;
        updateSlider(sliderPosition, container, overlay, handle);
        e.preventDefault();
        break;
    }
  });
}

/**
 * Update slider position
 */
function updateSlider(position, container, overlay, handle) {
  // Update overlay width
  overlay.style.width = `${position}%`;

  // Update handle position
  handle.style.left = `${position}%`;

  // Update ARIA attributes
  handle.setAttribute('aria-valuenow', Math.round(position));

  // Update background position for smooth image transition
  overlay.style.backgroundPosition = `${100 - position}% center`;
}

/**
 * Create a simple static comparison (fallback for browsers without JS)
 */
function createStaticComparison(container) {
  const beforeImage = container.querySelector('.before-image');
  const afterImage = container.querySelector('.after-image');

  if (!beforeImage || !afterImage) return;

  // Create a simple side-by-side layout
  container.style.display = 'flex';

  beforeImage.style.flex = '1';
  beforeImage.style.objectFit = 'cover';
  beforeImage.style.height = '300px';

  afterImage.style.flex = '1';
  afterImage.style.objectFit = 'cover';
  afterImage.style.height = '300px';

  // Add labels
  const beforeLabel = document.createElement('div');
  beforeLabel.textContent = 'Before';
  beforeLabel.style.textAlign = 'center';
  beforeLabel.style.padding = '0.5rem';
  beforeLabel.style.fontWeight = 'bold';

  const afterLabel = document.createElement('div');
  afterLabel.textContent = 'After';
  afterLabel.style.textAlign = 'center';
  afterLabel.style.padding = '0.5rem';
  afterLabel.style.fontWeight = 'bold';

  container.insertBefore(beforeLabel, beforeImage);
  container.appendChild(afterLabel);
}

// Export for potential use by other scripts
window.comparisonSlider = {
  initialize: initializeComparisonSliders,
  create: createComparisonSlider
};

/**
 * Properties 4 Creations - Forms Module
 * Handles form initialization and submission
 *
 * @fileoverview Initializes form functionality using validation module
 * @author Properties 4 Creations
 */

import { 
  handleApplicationSubmit, 
  handleContactSubmit, 
  addFormValidation, 
  setMinimumMoveInDate 
} from './validation.js';

/**
 * Initialize form validation and submission
 */
export function initForms() {
  // Set minimum date for move-in date field
  setMinimumMoveInDate();

  const forms = [
    document.getElementById('application-form'),
    document.getElementById('contact-form')
  ];

  forms.forEach(form => {
    if (form) {
      const submitButton = form.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
      if (submitButton) {
        submitButton.disabled = true; // Disable on page load
      }
      
      if (form.id === 'application-form') {
        form.addEventListener('submit', handleApplicationSubmit);
      } else if (form.id === 'contact-form') {
        form.addEventListener('submit', handleContactSubmit);
      }
      
      addFormValidation(form);
    }
  });
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Function to fetch and include HTML content
    function includeHTML() {
        // Load header
        fetch('/_header.html')
            .then(response => response.text())
            .then(data => {
                document.querySelector('body').insertAdjacentHTML('afterbegin', data);
            });

        // Load footer
        fetch('/_footer.html')
            .then(response => response.text())
            .then(data => {
                document.querySelector('body').insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', data);
            });
    }

    includeHTML();
});

/**

 * Main entry point with form validation and common functionality
 *
 * @fileoverview Initializes all JavaScript components and functionality
 * @author Properties 4 Creations
